<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***erven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:erven.html>erven</a> (11264)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:erven.html>erven</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*arbijaną</i>, denominative from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*arbiją</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃erbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">change allegiance or status or ownership</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erf.html>erf</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

***escapade.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:escapade.html>escapade</a> (51997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:escapade.html>escapade</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the act of escaping; a trick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">escapada</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">escapar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to escape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*excappō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to escape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with escape.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:escapade.html>escapade</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:escapades.html>escapades</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A daring or adventurous act; an undertaking which goes against convention.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1724</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Captain_Charles_Johnson" class="extiw" title="w:Captain Charles Johnson">Charles Johnson</a>,  “Of <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Howell_Davis" class="extiw" title="w:Howell Davis">Howel Davis</a>, and His Crew”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_General_History_of_the_Pyrates" class="extiw" title="w:A General History of the Pyrates">A General History of the Pyrates,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="from Their First Rise and Settlement in the Island of Providence, to the Present Time. With the Remarkable Actions and Adventures of the Two Female Pyrates Mary Read and Anne Bonny;  | ... |  To which is Added. A Short Abstract of the Statute and Civil Law, in Relation to Pyracy">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, 2nd edition, London |  Printed for, and <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> by <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Warner,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Black-Boy in Pater-Noster-Row">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/2276353">2276353</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/generalhistoryof00johnpage/202/mode/1up">page 202</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Manner of living among the <i>Portugueze</i> here <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, with the utmost Frugality and Temperance. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> The beſt of them (excepting the Governor now and then) neither pay nor receive any Viſits of <b>Eſcapade</b> or Recreation; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1816</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Scott" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Scott"><a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott</a>, <i>The Antiquary <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Volume II</i>, ch. 9:
<dl><dd>[Nobody] stood more confounded than Oldbuck at this sudden <b><a href = vnd.unilang:escapade.html>escapade</a></b> of his nephew. "<a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> the devil in him," <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> his first exclamation, "to go to disturb the <a href = vnd.unilang:brute.html>brute</a>?"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1918</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/P._G._Wodehouse" class="extiw" title="w:P. G. Wodehouse">P. G. Wodehouse</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:piccadilly.html>Piccadilly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jim.html>Jim</a></i>, ch. 1:

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:esdoorn.html>esdoorn</a> (42354)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">asdoren</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">es</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doorn.html>doorn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:esdoorn.html>esdoorn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:esdoorns.html>esdoorns</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">esdoornen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:esdoorn.html>esdoorntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">maple</span>, tree of the genus <i><span class="Latn" lang="mul">Acer</span></i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ahorn</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

Popper <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:monumentale.html>monumentale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reikwijdte.html>reikwijdte</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:charme.html>charme</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esprit.html>esprit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> merendeels <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstijgen.html>ontstijgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> salon- <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> gebruiksmuziek.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> | 5 | </a></sup> </i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***esquire.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a> (40846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">escuyer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">escuier</i>, properly, a shield-bearer (compare modern French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">écuyer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shield-bearer, armor-bearer, squire of a knight, <a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a>, equerry, rider, horseman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scutarius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shield-bearer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scutum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shield</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; probably akin to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hide</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">squire</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the result of apheresis. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">equerry</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">escutcheon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: solid aaa 1px; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="Wikipedia-logo.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/14px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/21px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/28px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 15px;">  <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/esquire" class="extiw" title="w:esquire"><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></a></b> on Wikipedia</div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">esquires</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A lawyer.</li>
<li>A male member of the <a href = vnd.unilang:gentry.html>gentry</a> ranking below a knight.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1596–1599</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_IV,_Part_2" class="extiw" title="w:Henry IV, Part 2">The Second Part of <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Fourth,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Containing His Death: And the Coronation of King Henry the Fift.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I am Robert Shallow, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>; a poor <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b> of the county, and one of the king's justices of the peace.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1875</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herbert_Broom" class="extiw" title="w:Herbert Broom">Herbert Broom</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Hadley" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Hadley">Edward Hadley</a>, notes by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Wait" class="extiw" title="w:William Wait">William Wait</a>, <i>Commentaries on the laws of England</i>, I-317:
<dl><dd><b>Esquires</b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:gentlemen.html>gentlemen</a> are confounded together by <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Coke" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Coke">Edward <a href = vnd.unilang:coke.html>Coke</a></a>, who observes that every <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a gentleman, and a gentleman <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> defined to be one <i>qui arma <a href = vnd.unilang:ritten.html>gerit</a></i>, who <a href = vnd.unilang:bears.html>bears</a> coat-armour, the grant of which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> thought to add gentility to a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s family. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indeed a matter somewhat unsettled what constitutes the distinction, or who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a real <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b>; for no estate, however large, per se confers this rank upon its owner.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">An honorific sometimes placed after a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s name.</span></li>
<li>A gentleman who attends or <a href = vnd.unilang:escorts.html>escorts</a> a lady in public.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A squire; a youth who in the hopes of becoming a knight attended upon a knight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A shield-bearer, but also applied to other attendants.
<ul><li><b>1801</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Strutt" class="extiw" title="w:Joseph Strutt">Joseph <a href = vnd.unilang:strutt.html>Strutt</a></a>, <i>The Sports and Pastimes of the People of England</i>
<dl><dd>The office of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b> consisted of several departments; the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b> for the body, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b> of the chamber, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b> of the stable, and the carving <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></b>; the latter stood in the hall at dinner, carved the different dishes, and distributed them to the guests.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In England this title <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> given to the eldest sons of knights, and the elder sons of the younger sons of peers and their eldest sons in succession, <a href = vnd.unilang:officers.html>officers</a> of the king's courts and of the household, barristers, justices of the peace while in commission, <a href = vnd.unilang:sheriffs.html>sheriffs</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gentlemen.html>gentlemen</a> who have <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> commissions in the army and navy, etc.: but opinions with regard to the correct usage vary. There are also esquires of knights of the Bath, each knight appointing three at his installation. The title now <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually conceded to all professional and literary <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>. In the United States the title <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> regarded as belonging especially to lawyers.</li>
<li>In legal and other formal documents <b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>Esquire</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually written in full after the names of those considered entitled to the designation; in common usage it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> abbreviated Esq. or Esqr., and appended to any <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s name as a <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a> mark of respect, as in the addresses of <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> (though this practice <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> becoming less prevalent than formerly). In the general sense, and as a title either alone or prefixed to a name, the form Squire <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> always <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> the more common in familiar use. <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <i>Century</i>, 1914</li>
<li>See also the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Esquire" class="extiw" title="w:Esquire">Wikipedia article on "<a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>Esquire</a>"</a></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>Esquire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> See <a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedel</a></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">esquires</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">esquiring</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">esquired</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To attend, wait on, escort.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">esquiere</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">esquierre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">esquarre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a square</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>esquire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">esquires</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bearing somewhat resembling a gyron, but extending across the field so that the point touches the opposite edge of the escutcheon.</li></ol>

***etage.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:etage.html>etage</a> (6200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">étage</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etage.html>etage</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etages.html>etages</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etage.html>etagetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>floor, storey</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In the Dutch-speaking countries, the first floor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the floor one level above ground level. The ground level <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begane.html>begane</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:etage.html>etage</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woonde.html>woonde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derde.html>derde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:etage.html>etage</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:flatgebouw.html>flatgebouw</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
